**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **itaratra svarge | iha bhārata-bhūmau punar api dharmādharmayor bhava utpattir yatas tasmin ubhayayoḥ dharmādharmayoḥ śeṣābhyām ||37||

—o)0(o—

**|| 5.26.38 ||**


    **nivṛtti-lakṣaṇa-mārga ādāv eva vyākhyātaḥ | etāvān evāṇḍa-kośo yaś caturdaśadhā purāṇeṣu vikalpita upagīyate yat tad bhagavato nārāyaṇasya sākṣān mahā-puruṣasya sthaviṣṭhaṁ rūpam ātmamāyā-guṇamayam anuvarṇitam ādṛtaḥ paṭhati śṛṇoti śrāvayati sa upageyaṁ bhagavataḥ paramātmano’grāhyam api śraddhā-bhakti-viśuddha-buddhir veda.**

**śrīdharaḥ : **ādāv eva dvitīya-skandhe vaiśvānaraṁ yāti[bhā.pu. 2.2.24] ity-ādinā | upageyam aupaniṣadaṁ rūpam | śraddha-bhaktibhyāṁ viśuddha buddhir yasya ||38||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **ādāv eva dvitīya-tṛtīyādiṣu vaiśvānaraṁ yāti[bhā.pu. 2.2.24] ity-ādibhiḥ | upageyam aupaniṣadaṁ rūpaṁ grahītum aśakyam ||38||

—o)0(o—

**|| 5.26.39 ||**


    **śrutvā sthūlaṁ tathā sūkṣmaṁ rūpaṁ bhagavato yatiḥ |**


    **sthūle nirjitam ātmānaṁ śanaiḥ sūkṣmaṁ dhiyā nayed iti ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **yathā yathāvac chrutvā ||39||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **yathā sthūlaṁ śrutvā tathā sūkṣmaṁ ca śrutvā, sthūle rūpe ātmānaṁ nirjitaṁ kṛtvā śanaiḥ krameṇa sūkṣmaṁ prati dhiyā vyavasāyātmikayā buddhyā nayed ity anvayaḥ | pāṭhāntaraṁ tu sugamam | sūkṣmam atra bhakti-mātra-gamyaṁ rūpaṁ—


        yavan na jāyeta parāvare’smin 


        viśveśvare draṣṭari bhakti-yogaḥ [bhā.pu. 2.2.14] iti dvitīyokteḥ ||39||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **yathā yathāvat sthūle rūpe nimajjitaṁ vaśīkṛtam ātmānaṁ manaḥ ||39||

—o)0(o—

**|| 5.26.40 ||**


    **bhū-dvīpa-varṣa-sarid-adri-nabhaḥ-samudra- **


    **pātāla-diṅ-naraka-bhāgaṇa-loka-saṁsthā |**


    **gītā mayā tava nṛpādbhutam īśvarasya**


    **sthūlaṁ vapuḥ sakala-jīva-nikāya-dhāma ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **kathaṁ-bhūtā saṁsthā ? sakalānāṁ jīva-nikāyānāṁ dhāma āśraya-bhūtaṁ vapuḥ ||40||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ, viśvanāthaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

iti sārārtha-darśinyāṁ harṣiṇyāṁ bhakta-cetasām |

ṣaḍviṁśaḥ pañcame skandhe saṅgataḥ saṅgataḥ satām ||*||

sahiṣṇutā-divya-sudhā-pravāhān

sādhūn samākarṇya jijīviṣāmi |

sva-dhārṣṭya-durvāra-bhujaṅga-daṣṭa-

syāho gatir me katham anyathā syāt ||

pañcama-skandha-ṭīkā śrī-rādhā-kṛṣṇa-saras-taṭe |

kṛṣṇa-ṣaṣṭhyām apurīyaṁ phālguna-bhauma-vāsare ||

—o)0(o—


    iti śrīmad-bhāgavate mahā-purāṇe brahma-sūtra-bhāṣye pāramahaṁsyaṁ saṁhitāyāṁ vaiyāsikyāṁ pañcama-skandhe 


    naraka-varṇanaṁ nāma ṣaḍviṁśo’dhyāyaḥ |

|| 5.26 ||

iti pañcama-skandhaḥ samāptaḥ

## Notes

[^1]:
    gṛhe ity upalakṣaṇaṁ dārāpatyādīnāṁ iti siddhāṁ.

[^2]:
    1.6.29 sārārtha-darśinī draṣṭavyā

[^3]:
    dvā suparṇā sayujā sakhāyā samānaṁ vṛkṣaṁ pariṣasvajāte |
    tayor anyaḥ pippalaṁ svādv atty anaśnann anyo’bhicākaśīti ||

[^4]:
    ayaṁ gadyaḥ kvacid dvi vibhaktaḥ. 

[^5]:
    caitanya-gauḍīya-maṭha-saṁskaraṇe atra viśvanāthasya adhyāya-samāpti-cihnaḥ “iti sārārtha-darśinyām” ity-ādi-śloko na prāpyate.

[^6]:
    tathāpi iti ga-gha-pustakayoḥ.

[^7]:
    keṣucit saṁskāreṣu kevalo’yam eva pāṭhaḥ: brahma-saukhyasya nirviśeṣa-saviśeṣatā-bhedena dvaividhya-pratipādakaṁ mahatāṁ dvaividhyam āha—sama-cittāḥ abheda-darśinaḥ | teṣāṁ sādhanāny āha—praśāntā ity-ādinā | uttareṣām api sādhanāny āha—janeṣv ity-ādinā | yāvān artho mat-sauhṛda-maya-bhaktiḥ, tāvān tad-anurūpa eva na tv adhika-nyūnaḥ, artho dhanaṁ yeṣāṁ te |_| _iti.

[^8]:
    tatra yādṛśaḥ sat-paricaryā-rūpaḥ sat-prasaṅgas tādṛśam eva para-tattva-sāmmukhyaṁ, tat-sarva-śreṣṭha-phalatvena  para-tattva-sākṣātkārātmaka-vimukti-lakṣaṇa-tad-vaśīkāratve ca paryavasīyate | asyāḥ [mahat-paricaryāyāḥ] śravaṇādi-saśraddha-sādhana-bhakti-yājnataḥ pūrvatvam āha—mahad ity ardhena || iti purī-dāsa-saṁskāre pāda-ṭīkā.

[^9]:
    tad-dhāraṇe ca iti purī-dāsa-nirvācita-pāṭhaḥ.

[^10]:
    nivṛttyā iti ṅa-pustake.

[^11]:
    tathānyeṣām apavargāṇām api tayā tiraskṛtau mukta-kaṇṭhā eva śabdā udāhāryāḥ | sā ca tiraskṛtiḥ kvacit tat-svarūpeṇa kriyate | kvacit tat-parikara-dvārā ca | tatra tat-svarūpeṇa tiraskṛtim āha gadyena—yasyām iti | ity adhika-pāṭhaḥ purī-dāsena na dhṛtaḥ. 

[^12]:
    yasya bhaktir bhagavati harau niḥśreyaseśvare
    vikrīḍato’mṛtāmbhodhau kiṁ kṣudraiḥ khātakodakaiḥ

[^13]:
    tam evābhimāna-mamatābhyāṁ prīter atiśayaṁ darśayati—iti prīti-sandarbhoktāvataraṇikā.

[^14]:
    śrī-bhagavad-viṣayaka-rati-pradatvam uktam | evaṁ nirjita-ṣaḍ-vargaiḥ kriyate bhaktir īśvare [bhā.pu. 7.7.33] ity-ādinā | iti bhakti-sandarbhe nimna-pradatta-vyākhyātaḥ pūrvaṁ likhitam.

[^15]:
    satyaṁ diśaty arthitam arthito nṛṇāṁ
    naivārthado yat punar arthitā yataḥ
    svayaṁ vidhatte bhajatām anicchatām
    icchāpidhānaṁ nija-pāda-pallavam

[^16]:
    ujjihāse iti pāṭhāntaram.

[^17]:
    yayā saṁmohito jīva ātmānaṁ triguṇātmakaṁ |
    paro’pi manute’narthaṁ tat-kṛtaṁ cābhipadyate || [bhā.pu. 1.7.5] iti |

[^18]:
    bhayaṁ dvitīyābhiniveśataḥ syād
    īśād apetasya viparyayo’smṛtiḥ |
    tan-māyayāto budha ābhajet taṁ
    bhaktyaikayeśaṁ guru-devatātmā ||

[^19]:
    sarva-kṣetrasya iti vividha-pāṇḍulipibhyaḥ purīdāsair dhṛtaḥ paramātma-sandarbha-pāṭhaḥ.

[^20]:
    bhagavato māyayā iti kha-pāṭhaḥ.

    nirdiṣṭatvāt (ṅa)
